				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Ich steh mit einem Fuß im Grabe, BWV 156 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>

<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1729 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Ich steh mit einem Fuß im Grabe
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">I stand with one foot in the grave
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 156&#160;; BC A 38
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 318
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>F major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 movements:
<ol><li> Sinfonia (sometimes titled "Arioso")
</li><li> Chorale (soprano) and Aria (tenor): Ich steh mit einem Fuß im Grabe
</li><li> Recitative (bass): Mein Angst und Not 
</li><li> Aria (alto): Herr, was du willt, soll mir gefallen
</li><li> Recitative (bass): Und willst du, dass ich nicht soll kranken 
</li><li> Chorale: Herr, wie du willt, so schicks mit mir
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1729 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1729-01-23 in Leipzig&#160;?
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1886 (BGA)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><i>see below</i>
<dl><dd><a href="/wiki/Category:Schein,_Johann_Hermann" title="Category:Schein, Johann Hermann">Johann Hermann Schein</a> (1586-1630) (No.2)<br /><a href="/wiki/Category:Henrici,_Christian_Friedrich" title="Category:Henrici, Christian Friedrich">Christian Friedrich Henrici</a> (1700-1764) (Nos.3-5), as Picander<br /><a href="/wiki/Category:Bienemann,_Kasper" title="Category:Bienemann, Kasper">Kasper Bienemann</a> (1540-1591) (No.6)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>German
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Dedication
</th>
<td>3rd Sunday after Epiphany
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque" title="Category:Baroque">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque_style" title="Category:Baroque style">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>

</th>
<td><i>Voices:</i> alto, tenor, bass, mixed chorus (SATB)<br /><i>Orchestra:</i> oboe, strings, continuo
